    - generic [ref=e36]:
      - paragraph [ref=e37]: This is the confirmed schedule of HXMT observations for SGR J1935+2154. Please note that the schedule is subject to change and the new schedule will be updated timely. The observation start (MNV=maneuver) time is in UTC and only the periods when the source is completely visible are listed, i.e., the source is not blocked by the earth and the satellite is not in SAA.
